 tippaniyan Researchers used a nationally representative sample of the 1950 Finnish census to reach conclusions

 It was found that the risk of death among those who become father at the age of 22 is 26 percent more than 25 or 26

 ' hamamen se zyaadaatar log apane din ke zyaadaatar ghante screen ke saamne baithkar bitaate hai
 Whether it is a computer screen or a mobile screen
 ghanton digital screen ke saamne baithne kaa sabase bura asar hamaari ankhon par padataa he
 Due to which the possibility of getting stress, insomnia and many other diseases increases
 ankhon se judi is takalif ko Digital Eye Strain kehete hai
 Digital Eye Strain was earlier known as computer vision syndrome
 yah beemaari din-pratidin logon main badhati hi ja rahi he
 Earlier only work was done on computer but now laptops, tablets, smart phones have also become an important part of our life
 in chizon ke bahut adhik istemaal se Digital Eye Strain kii problem ho jaati he
 It can start with mild eye pain
 lekin samay rahete ilaaj nahin karaayaa jaae to bhavishya main ankhon kii roshni bhi ja sakati he
 Early symptoms of Digital Eye Strain: The initial symptoms are eye strain, watery eyes, pain, blurred vision, redness
 iske saath hi sirdard or ghabrahat bhi ho sakati he
 Sometimes it can also be a cause of irritability
 ho saktaa he subah uthakar aapako takalif kam ho lekin din badhane ke saath hi ye takalif badhane lagati he
 Prevention and Treatment -1
 digital products kistemaal karnaa hamaari jarurat ban chuki he
 In such a situation, we should also know the right way to use them
 in chizon ko ankhon ke bahut paas yaa dur rakhkar yuj karnaa khatarnaak ho saktaa he
 These things should be used only by keeping them at a certain distance
 2
 There should be enough light in the room where you are using these things
 varanaa ankhon par jor padegaa
 3
 offis main asi vent ke saamne nahin baithna chahie
 This makes the eyes water dry
 20-20-20 kaa niyam follow karnaa chahie
 People who work long hours in computers and laptops in the office, they should watch every 20 minutes for 20 seconds on something kept at 20 feet away
 ye ankhon ke tanaav ko kam karata he
 4
 screenzyada brit nahin honi chahieor font sies bahut chote nahin hone chahie
 5
 jab aap der tak computer par kaam karte hai to aapaki palken ek minute main 6-8 baar hi jhapakati hai jabaki 16-18 baar palkon kaa jhapakna normal hota he
 In such a situation, it is necessary to have an eye checkup once every six months

 Governor of Goa
 shankaranarayan ne ramesh tawarkar, mahadev nike, dilip parulekar tathaa milind nike (sabhi bhartiya janata party) or pandurang urf deepak dhavlikar (maharashtravaadi gomantak party) evam avertino phutado (nirdaleey) ko pad evam gopneeyata kii shapath dilaai
 Four BJP ministers have been elected members of the 40-member assembly for the second time, while Deepak Dhavalikar's brother Sudin has been the first minister in the Goa government
 avertino phutado un do isai ummidavaaron main se ek hai jinhen march main hue chunaav main bhaajapa kaa samarthan praapt tha
 The comments mantrimandal main is vistaar ke saath bhaajapa ke netritv vaali gathbandhan sarkaar main mantriyon kii sankhya 11 ho gai jo adhiktam seemaa se ek kam he
 It is noteworthy that Parrikar along with five ministers was sworn in as Chief Minister on March 9 but a few days later Tourism Minister Mathani Saldanha died due to a heart attack
 goa ke rajyapal ke
 Shankaranarayan administered the oath of office and secrecy to Ramesh Tawadkar, Mahadev Naik, Dilip Parulekar and Milind Naik (all Bharatiya Janata Party) and Pandurang alias Deepak Dhavalikar (maharashtrawadi Gomantak Party) and Avertino Futado (independent)
 bhaajapa ke chaar mantri 40 sadasyeey vidhansabha ke duusari baar sadsy chune gaye hai jabaki deepak dhavlikar ke bhai sudin goa sarkaar main pehle mantri rah chuke hai
 Avertino Futado is one of the two Christian candidates who supported the BJP in the March election
